FROM [Chat] AS [c]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [u].[ChatsId], [u].[MembersId], [a].[Id], [a].[AccessFailedCount], [a].[Avatar], [a].[BirthDate], [a].[ConcurrencyStamp], [a].[Email], [a].[EmailConfirmed], [a].[Gender], [a].[LockoutEnabled], [a].[LockoutEnd], [a].[Name], [a].[NormalizedEmail], [a].[NormalizedUserName], [a].[PasswordHash], [a].[PhoneNumber], [a].[PhoneNumberConfirmed], [a].[SecurityStamp], [a].[TwoFactorEnabled], [a].[UserName]
    FROM [UserChats] AS [u]
    INNER JOIN [AspNetUsers] AS [a] ON [u].[MembersId] = [a].[Id]
) AS [t] ON [c].[Id] = [t].[ChatsId]
WHERE (
    SELECT COUNT(*)
    FROM [UserChats] AS [u0]
    INNER JOIN [AspNetUsers] AS [a0] ON [u0].[MembersId] = [a0].[Id]
    WHERE [c].[Id] = [u0].[ChatsId]) = @__Count_0
ORDER BY [c].[Id], [t].[ChatsId], [t].[MembersId], [t].[Id]

FROM [Chat] AS [c]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [t].[Id], [t].[Body], [t].[ChatId], [t].[CreationDate], [t].[SenderId]
    FROM (
        SELECT [m].[Id], [m].[Body], [m].[ChatId], [m].[CreationDate], [m].[SenderId], ROW_NUMBER() OVER(PARTITION BY [m].[ChatId] ORDER BY [m].[CreationDate] DESC) AS [row]
        FROM [Message] AS [m]
    ) AS [t]
    WHERE [t].[row] <= 1
) AS [t0] ON [c].[Id] = [t0].[ChatId]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [u].[ChatsId], [u].[MembersId], [a].[Id], [a].[AccessFailedCount], [a].[Avatar], [a].[BirthDate], [a].[ConcurrencyStamp], [a].[Email], [a].[EmailConfirmed], [a].[Gender], [a].[LockoutEnabled], [a].[LockoutEnd], [a].[Name], [a].[NormalizedEmail], [a].[NormalizedUserName], [a].[PasswordHash], [a].[PhoneNumber], [a].[PhoneNumberConfirmed], [a].[SecurityStamp], [a].[TwoFactorEnabled], [a].[UserName]
    FROM [UserChats] AS [u]
    INNER JOIN [AspNetUsers] AS [a] ON [u].[MembersId] = [a].[Id]
) AS [t1] ON [c].[Id] = [t1].[ChatsId]
WHERE EXISTS (
    SELECT 1
    FROM [UserChats] AS [u0]
    INNER JOIN [AspNetUsers] AS [a0] ON [u0].[MembersId] = [a0].[Id]

FROM [Chat] AS [c]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [t].[Id], [t].[Body], [t].[ChatId], [t].[CreationDate], [t].[SenderId]
    FROM (
        SELECT [m].[Id], [m].[Body], [m].[ChatId], [m].[CreationDate], [m].[SenderId], ROW_NUMBER() OVER(PARTITION BY [m].[ChatId] ORDER BY [m].[CreationDate] DESC) AS [row]
        FROM [Message] AS [m]
    ) AS [t]
    WHERE [t].[row] <= 1
) AS [t0] ON [c].[Id] = [t0].[ChatId]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [u].[ChatsId], [u].[MembersId], [a].[Id], [a].[AccessFailedCount], [a].[Avatar], [a].[BirthDate], [a].[ConcurrencyStamp], [a].[Email], [a].[EmailConfirmed], [a].[Gender], [a].[LockoutEnabled], [a].[LockoutEnd], [a].[Name], [a].[NormalizedEmail], [a].[NormalizedUserName], [a].[PasswordHash], [a].[PhoneNumber], [a].[PhoneNumberConfirmed], [a].[SecurityStamp], [a].[TwoFactorEnabled], [a].[UserName]
    FROM [UserChats] AS [u]
    INNER JOIN [AspNetUsers] AS [a] ON [u].[MembersId] = [a].[Id]
) AS [t1] ON [c].[Id] = [t1].[ChatsId]
WHERE EXISTS (
    SELECT 1
    FROM [UserChats] AS [u0]
    INNER JOIN [AspNetUsers] AS [a0] ON [u0].[MembersId] = [a0].[Id]
    WHERE ([c].[Id] = [u0].[ChatsId]) AND ([a0].[Id] = @__entity_equality_user_0_Id)) AND ((
    SELECT COUNT(*)
    FROM [Message] AS [m0]
    WHERE [c].[Id] = [m0].[ChatId]) > 0)
